398|579307|    // MARK: - API Request
399|b4687f|    
400|0a6144|    private func makeAPIRequest(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?) async throws -> String {
401|162b99|        switch selectedProvider {
402|6ca85d|        case .openai:
403|d9a528|            return try await callOpenAI(messages: messages, context: context)
404|2b5eb0|        case .anthropic:
405|afe61a|            return try await callAnthropic(messages: messages, context: context)
406|51e5bc|        case .google:
407|688f02|            return try await callGoogle(messages: messages, context: context)
408|a90b5c|        case .kimi:
409|467f79|            return try await callKimi(messages: messages, context: context)
410|448974|        case .glm:
411|d03556|            return try await callGLM(messages: messages, context: context)
412|6a2402|        case .groq:
413|2fdc7f|            return try await callGroq(messages: messages, context: context)
414|586fca|        case .deepseek:
415|b7290a|            return try await callDeepSeek(messages: messages, context: context)
416|0935ee|        case .mistral:
417|048202|            return try await callMistral(messages: messages, context: context)
418|7b8ebd|        case .ollama:
419|20a226|            return try await callOllama(messages: messages, context: context)
420|5f3077|        }
421|27e597|    }

423|b90399|    // MARK: - OpenAI API
424|b4687f|    
425|c4fdfa|    private func callOpenAI(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?) async throws -> String {
426|bc2d67|        let url = URL(string: "\(AIProvider.openai.baseURL)/chat/completions")!
427|6007aa|        var request = URLRequest(url: url)
428|89eca9|        request.httpMethod = "POST"
429|7fd512|        request.setValue("Bearer \(openAIKey)", forHTTPHeaderField: "Authorization")
430|0b9fcc|        request.setValue("application/json", forHTTPHeaderField: "Content-Type")
431|d6ed84|        
432|84a07c|        var apiMessages: [[String: String]] = []
433|d6ed84|        
434|5740dd|        // Add system message with context
435|fd71f7|        let systemPrompt = buildSystemPrompt(context: context)
436|55709b|        apiMessages.append(["role": "system", "content": systemPrompt])
437|d6ed84|        
438|c5ae63|        // Add conversation messages
439|0c7100|        for msg in messages {
440|89949c|            apiMessages.append(["role": msg.role.rawValue, "content": msg.content])
441|5f3077|        }
442|d6ed84|        
443|825e3e|        let body: [String: Any] = [
444|e981b8|            "model": selectedModel.id,
445|b5548e|            "messages": apiMessages,
446|d6271e|            "max_tokens": 4096,
447|f1c54d|            "temperature": 0.7
448|220505|        ]
449|d6ed84|        
450|bae13e|        request.httpBody = try JSONSerialization.data(withJSONObject: body)
451|d6ed84|        
452|57e527|        let (data, response) = try await URLSession.shared.data(for: request)
453|d6ed84|        
454|2748ab|        guard let httpResponse = response as? HTTPURLResponse else {
455|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
456|5f3077|        }
457|d6ed84|        
458|42034c|        if httpResponse.statusCode != 200 {
459|a214f5|            if let errorJson = try? JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: data) as? [String: Any],
460|3cebbe|               let error = errorJson["error"] as? [String: Any],
461|be8727|               let message = error["message"] as? String {
462|f87f3a|                throw AIError.apiError(message)
463|a7dc16|            }
464|6baa43|            throw AIError.httpError(httpResponse.statusCode)
465|5f3077|        }
466|d6ed84|        
467|c94159|        let json = try JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: data) as? [String: Any]
468|95fe6c|        guard let choices = json?["choices"] as? [[String: Any]],
469|6c7545|              let firstChoice = choices.first,
470|9e7d93|              let message = firstChoice["message"] as? [String: Any],
471|870b1f|              let content = message["content"] as? String else {
472|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
473|5f3077|        }
474|d6ed84|        
475|9be7b6|        return content
476|27e597|    }

523|31d41c|              let text = firstContent["text"] as? String else {
524|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
525|5f3077|        }

532|190d00|    private func callGoogle(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?) async throws -> String {

536|0b9fcc|        request.setValue("application/json", forHTTPHeaderField: "Content-Type")
537|d6ed84|

539|d6ed84|

542|e08e07|        parts.append(["text": "System: \(systemPrompt)"])
543|d6ed84|        
544|c1c8d4|        // Add messages
545|0c7100|        for msg in messages {
546|989b77|            let role = msg.role == .assistant ? "Model" : "User"
547|35f120|            parts.append(["text": "\(role): \(msg.content)"])
548|5f3077|        }
549|d6ed84|        
550|825e3e|        let body: [String: Any] = [
551|6251fc|            "contents": [
552|f76f20|                ["parts": parts]
553|97e7d5|            ],
554|0eaa6f|            "generationConfig": [
555|80d7f4|                "maxOutputTokens": 4096,
556|e772de|                "temperature": 0.7
557|324820|            ]
558|220505|        ]
559|d6ed84|        
560|bae13e|        request.httpBody = try JSONSerialization.data(withJSONObject: body)
561|d6ed84|        
562|57e527|        let (data, response) = try await URLSession.shared.data(for: request)
563|d6ed84|        
564|2748ab|        guard let httpResponse = response as? HTTPURLResponse else {
565|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
566|5f3077|        }
567|d6ed84|        
568|42034c|        if httpResponse.statusCode != 200 {
569|a214f5|            if let errorJson = try? JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: data) as? [String: Any],
570|3cebbe|               let error = errorJson["error"] as? [String: Any],
571|be8727|               let message = error["message"] as? String {
572|f87f3a|                throw AIError.apiError(message)
573|a7dc16|            }
574|6baa43|            throw AIError.httpError(httpResponse.statusCode)
575|5f3077|        }
576|d6ed84|        
577|c94159|        let json = try JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: data) as? [String: Any]
578|12af8b|        guard let candidates = json?["candidates"] as? [[String: Any]],
579|977b10|              let firstCandidate = candidates.first,
580|0ff2f5|              let content = firstCandidate["content"] as? [String: Any],
581|9ddaf9|              let parts = content["parts"] as? [[String: Any]],
582|61737e|              let firstPart = parts.first,
583|a6eafc|              let text = firstPart["text"] as? String else {
584|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
585|5f3077|        }
586|d6ed84|        
587|ec263c|        return text
588|27e597|    }

932|c53a51|    private func extractCodeBlocks(from text: String) -> [CodeBlock] {
933|791eb5|        var blocks: [CodeBlock] = []
934|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
935|d6ed84|        
936|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
937|f7ed63|            return blocks
938|5f3077|        }
939|d6ed84|        
940|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
941|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
942|d6ed84|        
943|847e6d|        for match in matches {
944|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
945|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
946|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
947|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
948|9e5c94|                blocks.append(CodeBlock(language: language.isEmpty ? "text" : language, code: code))
949|a7dc16|            }
950|5f3077|        }
951|d6ed84|        
952|db7106|        return blocks
953|27e597|    }

127|e66206|    /// Updates suggestions based on the current text and cursor.
128|2cbc84|    ///
129|d91771|    /// FEAT-046: extracts symbols from `text` and mixes them into the suggestion list.
130|785f23|    /// FEAT-047: adds a curated set of Swift stdlib completions.
131|6224c3|    func updateSuggestions(for text: String, cursorPosition: Int) {
132|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
133|97fb6b|        guard let context = completionContext(in: text, cursorPosition: safeCursor) else {
134|0efe98|            apply(items: [])
135|bef5d6|            return
136|5f3077|        }
137|adc83b|
138|c2e8b0|        let prefixLower = context.prefix.lowercased()
139|042f0f|        guard !prefixLower.isEmpty else {
140|bacf86|            // If user just typed a dot, show members even with empty prefix.
141|a46e04|            if context.isMemberCompletion, let base = context.memberBase {
142|c9f7f8|                let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
143|92798d|                let items = members.map { Suggestion(kind: .member, displayText: $0, score: 1000) }
144|0b887c|                apply(items: items)
145|f5a6eb|            } else {
146|4c73d4|                apply(items: [])
147|a7dc16|            }
148|bef5d6|            return
149|5f3077|        }
150|adc83b|
151|3e8861|        var candidates: [Suggestion] = []
152|adc83b|
153|67a42f|        // FEAT-046: current file symbols
154|f70c93|        let symbols = extractSymbols(from: text)
155|27a302|        candidates.append(contentsOf: symbols
156|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
157|9de4dd|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .symbol, displayText: $0, score: 900) })
158|adc83b|
159|5f2431|        // Keywords
160|1a6e20|        candidates.append(contentsOf: keywords
161|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
162|b40e7e|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .keyword, displayText: $0, score: 800) })
163|adc83b|
164|fcf131|        // FEAT-047: Swift stdlib (top level)
165|d76253|        candidates.append(contentsOf: stdlibTopLevel
166|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
167|3cfc84|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .stdlib, displayText: $0, score: 700) })
168|adc83b|
169|07fafa|        // Member completions (very small heuristic-based set)
170|7f874f|        if context.isMemberCompletion, let base = context.memberBase {
171|68d0ac|            let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
172|a69811|            candidates.append(contentsOf: members
173|585680|                .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
174|73995e|                .map { Suggestion(kind: .member, displayText: $0, score: 1000) })
175|5f3077|        }
176|adc83b|

178|673af4|        let merged = mergeAndSort(candidates)
179|678fc2|        apply(items: merged)
180|27e597|    }

207|85ca8d|    func commitCurrentSuggestion(into text: inout String, cursorPosition: inout Int) {
208|f15814|        guard let suggestion = suggestionItems[safe: selectedIndex], showSuggestions else { return }
209|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))

231|f6601a|    private func completionContext(in text: String, cursorPosition: Int) -> CompletionContext? {
232|4c2df9|        guard !text.isEmpty else { return nil }
233|d6ed84|        
234|42915b|        // Safety check: ensure cursorPosition is within bounds
235|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
236|1fae78|        let cursorIndex = text.index(text.startIndex, offsetBy: safeCursor)
237|adc83b|
238|5aebf3|        // Find start of current identifier (letters/digits/_).
239|39f169|        var start = cursorIndex
240|26ebb3|        while start > text.startIndex {
241|c5c76e|            let prev = text.index(before: start)
242|9f8a31|            if isIdentifierChar(text[prev]) {
243|1929f8|                start = prev
244|f5a6eb|            } else {
245|74cfd8|                break
246|a7dc16|            }
247|5f3077|        }
248|adc83b|
249|bf292f|        let prefix = String(text[start..<cursorIndex])
250|adc83b|
251|824562|        // Member completion if immediately preceded by '.'
252|e374b4|        var isMember = false
253|e47c72|        var memberBase: String? = nil
254|adc83b|
255|0c2c38|        if start > text.startIndex {
256|2aa058|            let dotIndex = text.index(before: start)
257|88bd65|            if text[dotIndex] == "." {
258|ca8397|                isMember = true
259|adc83b|
260|6f6689|                // Parse identifier before '.'
261|91f615|                var baseEnd = dotIndex

264|56e352|                    let prev = text.index(before: baseStart)

272|ce472b|                if !base.isEmpty {

278|081616|        return CompletionContext(prefix: prefix,

280|a50c25|                                 isMemberCompletion: isMember,
281|ee9636|                                 memberBase: memberBase)

284|818e4b|    private func isIdentifierChar(_ c: Character) -> Bool {
285|c233b9|        // Swift identifiers are more complex, but this is enough for basic autocomplete.
286|a164d4|        return c.isLetter || c.isNumber || c == "_"
287|27e597|    }

291|622249|        if let members = memberCompletions[base] { return members }

294|adc83b|
295|6ba6d8|    private func extractSymbols(from text: String) -> [String] {
296|1098cf|        // Very lightweight symbol extraction: looks for common declarations.
297|141450|        // Intentionally best-effort; keeps FEAT-046 self-contained.
298|f746d2|        var results = Set<String>()
299|adc83b|
300|f97d0d|        func addMatches(pattern: String) {
301|ca0afa|            guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []) else { return }
302|6c811f|            let ns = text as NSString
303|b25f5b|            let range = NSRange(location: 0, length: ns.length)
304|d25847|            regex.enumerateMatches(in: text, options: [], range: range) { match, _, _ in
305|14f5aa|                guard let match, match.numberOfRanges >= 2 else { return }
306|345d9a|                let nameRange = match.range(at: 1)
307|de56e8|                guard nameRange.location != NSNotFound else { return }
308|8989a1|                let name = ns.substring(with: nameRange)
309|66b469|                if !name.isEmpty { results.insert(name) }
310|a7dc16|            }
311|5f3077|        }
312|adc83b|
313|a1c515|        // func Foo
314|cd4071|        addMatches(pattern: "\\bfunc\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)")
315|5eaefb|        // class/struct/enum/protocol/typealias Foo
316|685691|        addMatches(pattern: "\\b(?:class|struct|enum|protocol|typealias)\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)")
317|3764b8|        // let/var foo (captures first name before : = , )
318|bbf05c|        addMatches(pattern: "\\b(?:let|var)\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)(?=\\s*[:=,])")
319|adc83b|
320|01a90c|        return results.sorted { $0.localizedCaseInsensitiveCompare($1) == .orderedAscending }
321|27e597|    }
322|adc83b|
323|1470f2|    private func mergeAndSort(_ items: [Suggestion]) -> [Suggestion] {
324|ff1146|        // Keep highest-scored entry per id.
325|f6e288|        var bestById: [String: Suggestion] = [:]
326|686171|        for item in items {
327|0701eb|            if let existing = bestById[item.id] {
328|d5a6de|                if item.score > existing.score {
329|763640|                    bestById[item.id] = item
330|4e2d32|                }
331|f5a6eb|            } else {
332|b949a2|                bestById[item.id] = item
333|a7dc16|            }
334|5f3077|        }
335|adc83b|
336|cfe5f9|        return bestById.values.sorted {
337|708c2d|            if $0.score != $1.score { return $0.score > $1.score }
338|e5aa71|            return $0.displayText.localizedCaseInsensitiveCompare($1.displayText) == .orderedAscending
339|5f3077|        }
340|27e597|    }
341|adc83b|
342|ba218c|    private func apply(items: [Suggestion]) {
343|02d13b|        suggestionItems = items
344|f6da05|        suggestions = items.map { $0.displayText }
345|c77b90|        showSuggestions = !items.isEmpty
346|81a6a8|        selectedIndex = 0
347|27e597|    }
